)@@G@@*[@@@@*SDFF*:@@@@ @[@@@@ .    :@@@@E@G@@@@ . C$WAIT IS A UTILITIY WHICH KD
)@@G@@CAN BE CALLED FROM A FORTRAN (FTN) PROGRAM:@@@@O@G@@@@ . TO DO AN ER TO KE
)@@G@@TWAIT$; THIS WILL RESULT IN THE PROGRAM WAITING FOR A :@@@@Y@G@@@@ . PERKF
)@@G@@IOD OF ANYWHERE FROM 2 TO 30 SECONDS.  THE LENGTH OF THE WAIT     :@@@@*KG
)@@G@@@G@@@@ . SHOULD BE SENT AS A SINGLE ARGUMENT TO THE UTILITY, AND MUST BEKH
)@@G@@ AN   :@@@@2@G@@@@ . INTEGER.  IF THE INTEGER IS LESS THAN 2 OR GREATER KI
)@@G@@THAN 34359738, NO :@@@@/@G@@@@ . WAIT WILL OCCUR.  AN INTEGER BETWEEN 30KJ
)@@G@@ AND 34359738 WILL BE TREATED :@@@[[@G@@@@ . AS IF IT WERE 30.  IF THE NKK
)@@G@@UMBER IS NEGATIVE OR IS A DATA TYPE OTHER :@@@[A@G@@@@ . THAN INTEGER, RKL

)@@G@@A WAIT OF 30 SECONDS.                                                 P KN

)@@G@@C     :@@@]G@^@@@@      ITER=TGTDAY-WKDAY :@@@]L@ @@@@      IF (ITER.EQ.VG
)@@G@@0) RETURN   :@@@]Q@A@@@@      IF (ITER.LT.0) ITER=ITER+7    :@@@]U@[@@@@VH
)@@G@@C     :@@@]V@B@@@@C  MOVE FORWARD # OF DAYS TO TARGET DATE  :@@@]W@[@@@@VI
)@@G@@C     :@@@])@^@@@@      DO 10 I=1,ITER    :@@@]%@A@@@@         CALL TOMRVJ
)@@G@@OW (TGTDAT,DUMMY) :@@@]4@^@@@@         TGTDAT=DUMMY   :@@@]"@#@@@@10    VK
)@@G@@CONTINUE    :@@@#C@]@@@@      RETURN:@@@#M@]@@@@      END   _@@@@@C9@6.1VL
)@@G@@&'0)@[B,0@CSC9K@N3*@@@[#/K@@N\R'0BAKR];@@@C[@@@F;D@@@M/[F@@@B,;@@@C8)BAKVM
)@@G@@C@I@@]/,0@&$/K@@N(F[KELM*[@@@@*SDFF*:@@@@E@[@@@@C     :@@@@O@G@@@@C  THIVN
)@@G@@S SUBROUTINE ACCEPTS TODAYS DATE (CHARACTER*6) AND THE DAY OF THE :@@@@YVO
)@@G@@@G@@@@C  MONTH OF THE TARGET DATE (INTEGER) AND RETURNS THE NEXT DATE (YVP
)@@G@@YMMDD):@@@@*@G@@@@C  WHEN THAT DAY OF THE MONTH WILL OCCUR.  (IF TODAY IVQ
)@@G@@S THE 10TH OF MAY :@@@@2@G@@@@C  1988, AND THE DAY OF MONTH IS 02, THEN VR
)@@G@@THE DATE RETURNED WILL BE     :@@@@/@G@@@@C  880602 (CHARACTER*6).)  IF VS
)@@G@@THE DATE IS GREATER THAN THE LAST DATE OF :@@@[[@F@@@@C  THE MONTH, THE VT
)@@G@@LAST DATE OF THE MONTH WILL BE SUBSTITUTED.     :@@@[A@[@@@@C     :@@@[=VU
)@@G@@@C@@@@      SUBROUTINE FDTDAT(TODAY,TGTDAY,TGTDAT)    :@@@[(@ @@@@      VV
)@@G@@IMPLICIT INTEGER (A-Z)  :@@@[,@C@@@@      CHARACTER*6 TODAY,TGTDAT,DUMMYVW
)@@G@@,ENDMTH     :@@@[8@C@@@@      READ(UNIT=TODAY(5:6),FMT='(I2)')MTHDAY    VX
)@@G@@:@@@[.@#@@@@      TGTDAT=TODAY:@@@]]@A@@@@      IF (TGTDAY.LT.MTHDAY) THVY
)@@G@@EN    :@@@]G@C@@@@         READ(UNIT=TODAY,FMT='(2I2)')YEAR,MONTH :@@@]QVZ
)@@G@@@^@@@@         MONTH=MONTH+1  :@@@])@ @@@@         IF (MONTH.GT.12) THENWA
)@@G@@:@@@]%@^@@@@            YEAR=YEAR+1 :@@@]4@^@@@@            MONTH=1     WB
)@@G@@:@@@]"@#@@@@         ENDIF    :@@@##@D@@@@         WRITE(UNIT=TGTDAT(1:4WC
)@@G@@),FMT='(2J2)')YEAR,MONTH:@@@#C@]@@@@      ENDIF :@@@#M@C@@@@      WRITE(WD
)@@G@@UNIT=TGTDAT(5:6),FMT='(J2)')TGTDAY  :@@@#W@ @@@@      IF(TGTDAY.GT.28) TWE
)@@G@@HEN   :@@@#&@A@@@@         DUMMY=ENDMTH(TGTDAT(1:4))  :@@@#0@B@@@@      WF
)@@G@@   IF (DUMMY.LT.TGTDAT)TGTDAT=DUMMY :@@@#'@]@@@@      ENDIF :@@@^^@]@@@@WG
)@@G@@      RETURN:@@@^I@]@@@@      END   _@@@@@C@?@@]C80A72C[G@@@/\K@Y'/,0@GAWH

)@@G@@UM,STRING)  :@@@[,@[@@@@C     :@@@[8@D@@@@C  THIS SUBROUTINE WILL RETURNCO
)@@G@@ TO THE CALLING PROGRAM :@@@]]@D@@@@C  IN 'STRING' ANY OPTIONS THAT WERECP
)@@G@@ SPECIFIED IN THE :@@@]G@E@@@@C  @XQT STATEMENT WHICH CALLED THE PROGRAMCQ
)@@G@@, AND IN 'NUM,'   :@@@]L@C@@@@C  THE NUMBER OF OPTIONS SPECIFIED.  THE OCR
)@@G@@PTIONS:@@@]Q@D@@@@C  WILL BE IN ALPHABETICAL ORDER AND WILL INCLUDE ANY CS
)@@G@@:@@@])@A@@@@C  ALPHA CHARACTERS FROM A TO Z.    :@@@]%@[@@@@C     :@@@]4CT

)@@G@@RACTER*26.  CRU*FTNLIB MUST ALSO BE LIBED IN THE MAP. @E@@@[C  CHARACTERCX

)@@G@@G     :@@@#'@ @@@@      CHARACTER*1 LETTER(26)  :@@@^^@G@@@@      DATA LDA

)@@G@@:@@@ @@F@@@@C   INTERPRET THE BITS AND PREPARE THE CHARACTER STRING TO RDF
)@@G@@ETURN :@@@ E@ @@@@C   TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.   :@@@ O@[@@@@C     :@@@ YDG
)@@G@@@]@@@@      POS=1 :@@@ *@#@@@@      DO 20 I=1,26:@@@ 2@#@@@@         II=DH
)@@G@@I+10  :@@@ /@ @@@@         X=BITS(OPTNS,II,1)   :@@@AA@^@@@@         IF(DI
